Beyonce (feat. Jay-Z): Crazy In Love</title><content type='html'>&lt;a onblur=&quot;try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}&quot; href=&quot;http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_TDXdcf6kwqM/Sy6masy7S4I/AAAAAAAADXA/Y-rP1S7xJb4/s1600-h/B.jpg&quot;&gt;&lt;img style=&quot;margin: 0pt 0pt 10px 10px; float: right; cursor: pointer; width: 200px; height: 200px;&quot; src=&quot;http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_TDXdcf6kwqM/Sy6masy7S4I/AAAAAAAADXA/Y-rP1S7xJb4/s200/B.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; id=&quot;BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5417450379404856194&quot; border=&quot;0&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;Found on: &lt;span style=&quot;font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;Dangerously In Love&lt;/span&gt; (2003)&lt;br /&gt;Picked by: RN, MT, TF, WA, PA&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I&#39;ve listened to this song literally dozens of times, and I just finally realized how disjointed it is. One one hand you&#39;ve got Beyonce singing about how great her man is and how she&#39;s so head over heels in love that her sanity is actually in question. Then Jay-Z, the object of her obsession, comes in for a rap, and instead of returning the favor by lavishing her with praise he spends 40 seconds bragging about himself. Not cool, Jay. Pop Idol ceased production in 2003 and was replaced by a nearly identical show called The X Factor, which also features Simon Cowell.
